{file}") if json_files: print(f"\n📄 JSON FILES (likely containing structured data):") for file in json_files: print(f" - {file}") # Inspect the first JSON file that might contain our target data target_json = None for file in json_files: if 'scientific' in file.lower() or 'nano' in file.lower() or '2012' in file: target_json = file break if not target_json and json_files: target_json = json_files[0] # Take the first JSON file if no specific match if target_json: print(f"\n🔍 INSPECTING STRUCTURE OF: {target_json}") print("-" * 60) try: with open(f'workspace/{target_json}', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: data = json.load(f) print(f"File type: JSON") print(f"Top-level structure type: {type(data)}") if isinstance(data, dict): print(f"Top-level keys: {list(data.keys())}") # Look for keys that might contain article data for key in data.keys(): value = data[key] print(f" - {key}: {type(value)}") if isinstance(value, list): print(f" List length: {len(value)}") if len(value) > 0: print(f" First item type: {type(value[0])}") if isinstance(value[0], dict): print(f" Sample item keys: {list(value[0].keys())[:5]}") elif isinstance(value, dict): print(f" Dict keys: {list(value.keys())[:5]}") elif isinstance(value, str): print(f" String length: {len(value)}") print(f" Preview: {value[:100]}...") elif isinstance(data, list): print(f"List length: {len(data)}") if len(data) > 0: print(f"First item type: {type(data[0])}") if isinstance(data[0], dict): print(f"Sample item keys: {list(data[0].keys())}") # If this looks like article data, show a sample sample = data[0] if 'title' in sample or 'doi' in sample or 'abstract' in sample: print(f"\n📋 SAMPLE ARTICLE DATA STRUCTURE:") for key, value in sample.items(): if isinstance(value, str): print(f" {key}: {value[:100]}...") else: print(f" {key}: {type(value)} - {value}") except json.JSONDecodeError as e: print(f"Error reading JSON file: {e}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error inspecting file: {e}") # Look for any files that might contain the 23 articles mentioned in the PLAN print(f"\n🎯 SEARCHING FOR FILES CONTAINING '23' ARTICLES:") potential_article_files = [] for file in workspace_files: if any(term in file.lower() for term in ['article', 'paper', 'scientific', 'report', '2012']): potential_article_files.append(file) if potential_article_files: print(f"Potential article-containing files:") for file in potential_article_files: print(f" - {file}") else: print("No obvious article-containing files found based on filename patterns.") else: print("No workspace directory found.") print(f"\n{'='*80}") print("WORKSPACE INSPECTION COMPLETE") print(f"{'='*80}") print("Next step: Load and analyze the identified file containing the 23 Scientific Reports 2012 articles.")

import os import json from datetime import datetime # Fix the variable scope issue and properly examine workspace files print("Examining workspace directory structure...") print("=" * 80) if os.path.exists('workspace'): workspace_files = os.listdir('workspace') print(f"Total files in workspace: {len(workspace_files)}") print("\nFiles found:") # Categorize files by type and relevance to Scientific Reports 2012 scientific_reports_files = [] json_files = [] other_files = [] for filename in workspace_files: # Use 'filename' to avoid scope conflicts file_path = f'workspace/{filename}' file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path) print(f" - {filename} ({file_size:,} bytes)") if 'scientific' in filename.lower() and '2012' in filename: scientific_reports_files.append(filename) if filename.endswith('.json'): json_files.append(filename) if not filename.endswith('.json') and not ('scientific' in filename.lower() and '2012' in filename): other_files.append(filename) print(f"\nFile categorization:") print(f"Scientific Reports 2012 related: {len(scientific_reports_files)}") print(f"JSON files: {len(json_files)}") print(f"Other files: {len(other_files)}") # Focus on the largest JSON file which likely contains the article data if json_files: print(f"\n📄 JSON FILES ANALYSIS:") json_file_info = [] for json_file in json_files: file_path = f'workspace/{json_file}' file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path) json_file_info.append((json_file, file_size)) print(f" - {json_file}: {file_size:,} bytes") # Sort by size to identify the most comprehensive file json_file_info.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True) target_json = json_file_info[0][0] # Largest JSON file print(f"\n🔍 INSPECTING STRUCTURE OF LARGEST JSON FILE: {target_json}") print("-" * 60) try: with open(f'workspace/{target_json}', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: data = json.load(f) print(f"File type: JSON") print(f"Top-level structure type: {type(data)}") if isinstance(data, dict): print(f"Top-level keys: {list(data.keys())}") # Look for keys that might contain article data for key in data.keys(): value = data[key] print(f"\n Key '{key}': {type(value)}") if isinstance(value, list): print(f" List length: {len(value)}") if len(value) > 0: print(f" First item type: {type(value[0])}") if isinstance(value[0], dict) and len(value[0]) > 0: sample_keys = list(value[0].keys())[:5] print(f" Sample item keys: {sample_keys}") # Check if this looks like article data article_indicators = ['title', 'doi', 'abstract', 'authors', 'url', 'content'] matching_indicators = [k for k in sample_keys if k.lower() in [ind.lower() for ind in article_indicators]] if matching_indicators: print(f" ⭐ ARTICLE DATA INDICATORS FOUND: {matching_indicators}") elif isinstance(value, dict): dict_keys = list(value.keys())[:5] print(f" Dict keys: {dict_keys}") elif isinstance(value, str): print(f" String length: {len(value)}") if len(value) > 0: preview = value[:100].replace('\n', ' ').replace('\t', ' ') print(f" Preview: {preview}...") elif isinstance(data, list): print(f"List length: {len(data)}") if len(data) > 0: print(f"First item type: {type(data[0])}") if isinstance(data[0], dict): sample_keys = list(data[0].keys()) print(f"Sample item keys: {sample_keys}") # Check for article-like structure article_indicators = ['title', 'doi', 'abstract', 'authors', 'url', 'content'] matching_indicators = [k for k in sample_keys if k.lower() in [ind.lower() for ind in article_indicators]] if matching_indicators: print(f"\n📋 ARTICLE DATA STRUCTURE DETECTED!") print(f"Matching indicators: {matching_indicators}") # Show sample data structure sample = data[0] for key, value in sample.items(): if isinstance(value, str): preview = value[:150].replace('\n', ' ').replace('\t', ' ') print(f" {key}: {preview}...") else: print(f" {key}: {type(value)} - {value}") except json.JSONDecodeError as e: print(f"Error reading JSON file: {e}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error inspecting file: {e}") # Also check the text files for summary information print(f"\n📄 TEXT FILES ANALYSIS:") text_files = [f for f in workspace_files if f.endswith('.txt')] for txt_file in text_files: print(f"\n🔍 INSPECTING: {txt_file}") print("-" * 40) try: with open(f'workspace/{txt_file}', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: content = f.read() print(f"File size: {len(content):,} characters") print(f"First 300 characters:") preview = content[:300].replace('\n', '\n ') print(f" {preview}...") # Look for mentions of '23' articles or nano-compounds if '23' in content: print(f"\n⭐ CONTAINS '23' REFERENCE - likely mentions the target articles") if any(term in content.lower() for term in ['nano', 'compound', 'plasmon']): print(f"\n⭐ CONTAINS NANO-COMPOUND REFERENCES") except Exception as e: print(f"Error reading text file: {e}") else: print("No workspace directory found.") print(f"\n{'='*80}") print("WORKSPACE STRUCTURE ANALYSIS COMPLETE") print(f"{'='*80}") print("\nNext step: Load the identified JSON file containing article data and extract the 23 target articles.")

Python Code python
import os import json from datetime import datetime # Load the largest JSON file containing the detailed search results print("Loading Scientific Reports 2012 search results...") print("=" * 80) target_file = 'workspace/nature_scientific_reports_2012_search_results_20250806_163939.json' if os.path.exists(target_file): with open(target_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: search_data = json.load(f) print(f"✅ Successfully loaded: {target_file}") print(f"Search timestamp: {search_data.get('search_timestamp', 'N/A')}") print(f"Search focus: {search_data.get('search_focus', 'N/A')}") print(f"Total queries executed: {search_data.get('total_queries', 'N/A')}") print(f"Total results found: {search_data.get('total_results', 'N/A')}") # Extract the detailed results which should contain the article data detailed_results = search_data.get('detailed_results', []) print(f"\n📊 DETAILED RESULTS ANALYSIS:") print(f"Number of result sets: {len(detailed_results)}") # Collect all articles from all search result sets all_articles = [] for i, result_set in enumerate(detailed_results, 1): query = result_set.get('query', 'Unknown query') results = result_set.get('results', []) print(f"\n Result Set {i}:") print(f" Query: {query}") print(f" Articles found: {len(results)}") # Add articles to our collection for article in results: # Add query context to each article for tracking article_with_context = article.copy() article_with_context['source_query'] = query article_with_context['result_set'] = i all_articles.append(article_with_context) print(f"\n📚 TOTAL ARTICLES COLLECTED: {len(all_articles)}") print("=" * 80) # Now examine the structure of individual articles if all_articles: print(f"\n🔍 ARTICLE STRUCTURE ANALYSIS:") sample_article = all_articles[0] print(f"Sample article keys: {list(sample_article.keys())}") # Display key information from the first few articles print(f"\n📋 FIRST 5 ARTICLES OVERVIEW:") print("-" * 60) for i, article in enumerate(all_articles[:5], 1): title = article.get('title', 'No title') link = article.get('link', 'No URL') snippet = article.get('snippet', 'No snippet') print(f"\n Article {i}:") print(f" Title: {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") print(f" Snippet: {snippet[:200]}...") # Check if this appears to be a 2012 Scientific Reports article combined_text = f"{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()} {link.lower()}" indicators = { '2012': '2012' in combined_text, 'scientific reports': 'scientific reports' in combined_text or 'sci rep' in combined_text, 'nature': 'nature.com' in combined_text or 'nature' in combined_text, 'nano': any(term in combined_text for term in ['nano', 'nanoparticle', 'nanoscale', 'nanotube']), 'plasmon': any(term in combined_text for term in ['plasmon', 'plasmonic']) } print(f" Indicators: ", end="") for indicator, present in indicators.items(): if present: if indicator == 'plasmon': print(f"❌{indicator} ", end="") # We want articles WITHOUT plasmons else: print(f"✅{indicator} ", end="") print() # New line print(f"\n" + "=" * 80) print("FILTERING FOR TARGET ARTICLES") print("=" * 80) # Filter for 2012 Scientific Reports articles studying nano-compounds WITHOUT plasmon mentions target_articles = [] for article in all_articles: title = article.get('title', '') snippet = article.get('snippet', '') link = article.get('link', '') combined_text = f"{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()} {link.lower()}" # Check criteria is_2012 = '2012' in combined_text is_scientific_reports = ('scientific reports' in combined_text or 'sci rep' in combined_text or 'nature.com/srep' in combined_text or 'nature.com/articles/srep' in combined_text) has_nano_compound = any(term in combined_text for term in [ 'nano', 'nanoparticle', 'nanoscale', 'nanotube', 'nanostructure', 'nanocomposite', 'nanomaterial', 'quantum dot', 'graphene' ]) has_plasmon = any(term in combined_text for term in ['plasmon', 'plasmonic']) # Article must be 2012 Scientific Reports with nano-compounds but WITHOUT plasmons if is_2012 and is_scientific_reports and has_nano_compound and not has_plasmon: target_articles.append({ 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'source_query': article.get('source_query', ''), 'result_set': article.get('result_set', 0), 'criteria_met': { '2012': is_2012, 'scientific_reports': is_scientific_reports, 'nano_compound': has_nano_compound, 'no_plasmon': not has_plasmon } }) print(f"\n🎯 TARGET ARTICLES IDENTIFIED: {len(target_articles)}") if target_articles: print(f"\n📋 TARGET ARTICLES LIST:") print("-" * 80) for i, article in enumerate(target_articles, 1): print(f"\n {i}. {article['title']}") print(f" URL: {article['link']}") print(f" Snippet: {article['snippet'][:250]}...") print(f" Criteria: {article['criteria_met']}") # import os import json from datetime import datetime # Load the largest JSON file containing the detailed search results print("Loading Scientific Reports 2012 search results...") print("=" * 80) target_file = 'workspace/nature_scientific_reports_2012_search_results_20250806_163939.json' if os.path.exists(target_file): with open(target_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: search_data = json.load(f) print(f"✅ Successfully loaded: {target_file}") print(f"Search timestamp: {search_data.get('search_timestamp', 'N/A')}") print(f"Search focus: {search_data.get('search_focus', 'N/A')}") print(f"Total queries executed: {search_data.get('total_queries', 'N/A')}") print(f"Total results found: {search_data.get('total_results', 'N/A')}") # Extract the detailed results which should contain the article data detailed_results = search_data.get('detailed_results', []) print(f"\n📊 DETAILED RESULTS ANALYSIS:") print(f"Number of result sets: {len(detailed_results)}") # Collect all articles from all search result sets all_articles = [] for i, result_set in enumerate(detailed_results, 1): query = result_set.get('query', 'Unknown query') results = result_set.get('results', []) print(f"\n Result Set {i}:") print(f" Query: {query}") print(f" Articles found: {len(results)}") # Add articles to our collection for article in results: # Add query context to each article for tracking article_with_context = article.copy() article_with_context['source_query'] = query article_with_context['result_set'] = i all_articles.append(article_with_context) print(f"\n📚 TOTAL ARTICLES COLLECTED: {len(all_articles)}") print("=" * 80) # Now examine the structure of individual articles if all_articles: print(f"\n🔍 ARTICLE STRUCTURE ANALYSIS:") sample_article = all_articles[0] print(f"Sample article keys: {list(sample_article.keys())}") # Display key information from the first few articles print(f"\n📋 FIRST 5 ARTICLES OVERVIEW:") print("-" * 60) for i, article in enumerate(all_articles[:5], 1): title = article.get('title', 'No title') link = article.get('link', 'No URL') snippet = article.get('snippet', 'No snippet') print(f"\n Article {i}:") print(f" Title: {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") print(f" Snippet: {snippet[:200]}...") # Check if this appears to be a 2012 Scientific Reports article combined_text = f"{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()} {link.lower()}" indicators = { '2012': '2012' in combined_text, 'scientific reports': 'scientific reports' in combined_text or 'sci rep' in combined_text, 'nature': 'nature.com' in combined_text or 'nature' in combined_text, 'nano': any(term in combined_text for term in ['nano', 'nanoparticle', 'nanoscale', 'nanotube']), 'plasmon': any(term in combined_text for term in ['plasmon', 'plasmonic']) } print(f" Indicators: ", end="") for indicator, present in indicators.items(): if present: if indicator == 'plasmon': print(f"❌{indicator} ", end="") # We want articles WITHOUT plasmons else: print(f"✅{indicator} ", end="") print() # New line print(f"\n" + "=" * 80) print("FILTERING FOR TARGET ARTICLES") print("=" * 80) # Filter for 2012 Scientific Reports articles studying nano-compounds WITHOUT plasmon mentions target_articles = [] for article in all_articles: title = article.get('title', '') snippet = article.get('snippet', '') link = article.get('link', '') combined_text = f"{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()} {link.lower()}" # Check criteria is_2012 = '2012' in combined_text is_scientific_reports = ('scientific reports' in combined_text or 'sci rep' in combined_text or 'nature.com/srep' in combined_text or 'nature.com/articles/srep' in combined_text) has_nano_compound = any(term in combined_text for term in [ 'nano', 'nanoparticle', 'nanoscale', 'nanotube', 'nanostructure', 'nanocomposite', 'nanomaterial', 'quantum dot', 'graphene' ]) has_plasmon = any(term in combined_text for term in ['plasmon', 'plasmonic']) # Article must be 2012 Scientific Reports with nano-compounds but WITHOUT plasmons if is_2012 and is_scientific_reports and has_nano_compound and not has_plasmon: target_articles.append({ 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'source_query': article.get('source_query', ''), 'result_set': article.get('result_set', 0), 'criteria_met': { '2012': is_2012, 'scientific_reports': is_scientific_reports, 'nano_compound': has_nano_compound, 'no_plasmon': not has_plasmon } }) print(f"\n🎯 TARGET ARTICLES IDENTIFIED: {len(target_articles)}") if target_articles: print(f"\n📋 TARGET ARTICLES LIST:") print("-" * 80) for i, article in enumerate(target_articles, 1): print(f"\n {i}. {article['title']}") print(f" URL: {article['link']}") print(f" Snippet: {article['snippet'][:250]}...") print(f" Criteria: {article['criteria_met']}") # Python Code python
import os import json from datetime import datetime # Fix the variable scope issue and properly filter the Scientific Reports 2012 articles print("Loading and filtering Scientific Reports 2012 articles...") print("=" * 80) target_file = 'workspace/nature_scientific_reports_2012_search_results_20250806_163939.json' if os.path.exists(target_file): with open(target_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: search_data = json.load(f) print(f"✅ Successfully loaded: {target_file}") print(f"Search timestamp: {search_data.get('search_timestamp', 'N/A')}") print(f"Total queries executed: {search_data.get('total_queries', 'N/A')}") print(f"Total results found: {search_data.get('total_results', 'N/A')}") # Extract the detailed results which should contain the article data detailed_results = search_data.get('detailed_results', []) print(f"\n📊 DETAILED RESULTS ANALYSIS:") print(f"Number of result sets: {len(detailed_results)}") # Collect all articles from all search result sets all_articles = [] for i, result_set in enumerate(detailed_results, 1): query = result_set.get('query', 'Unknown query') results = result_set.get('results', []) print(f"\n Result Set {i}: {len(results)} articles") print(f" Query: {query}") # Add articles to our collection with context for article in results: article_with_context = article.copy() article_with_context['source_query'] = query article_with_context['result_set'] = i all_articles.append(article_with_context) print(f"\n📚 TOTAL ARTICLES COLLECTED: {len(all_articles)}") print("=" * 80) # Now filter for target articles (2012 Scientific Reports with nano-compounds, no plasmons) print(f"\n🔍 FILTERING FOR TARGET ARTICLES:") print("Criteria: 2012 + Scientific Reports + nano-compounds + NO plasmons") print("-" * 60) target_articles = [] for idx, article in enumerate(all_articles, 1): title = article.get('title', '') snippet = article.get('snippet', '') link = article.get('link', '') # Create combined text for analysis (fix variable scope issue) combined_text = f"{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()} {link.lower()}" # Check filtering criteria is_2012 = '2012' in combined_text is_scientific_reports = ( 'scientific reports' in combined_text or 'sci rep' in combined_text or 'nature.com/srep' in combined_text or 'nature.com/articles/srep' in combined_text or 'nature.com/subjects' in combined_text ) # Check for nano-compound terms nano_terms = [ 'nano', 'nanoparticle', 'nanoscale', 'nanotube', 'nanostructure', 'nanocomposite', 'nanomaterial', 'quantum dot', 'graphene', 'nanocrystal', 'nanowire', 'nanorod', 'nanosheet', 'fullerene' ] has_nano_compound = any(term in combined_text for term in nano_terms) # Check for plasmon terms (we want articles WITHOUT these) plasmon_terms = ['plasmon', 'plasmonic'] has_plasmon = any(term in combined_text for term in plasmon_terms) # Apply filtering criteria meets_criteria = is_2012 and is_scientific_reports and has_nano_compound and not has_plasmon if meets_criteria: # Find which nano terms matched matching_nano_terms = [term for term in nano_terms if term in combined_text] target_articles.append({ 'article_id': len(target_articles) + 1, 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'source_query': article.get('source_query', ''), 'result_set': article.get('result_set', 0), 'matching_nano_terms': matching_nano_terms, 'criteria_met': { '2012': is_2012, 'scientific_reports': is_scientific_reports, 'nano_compound': has_nano_compound, 'no_plasmon': not has_plasmon } }) print(f"✅ Article {len(target_articles)}: {title[:60]}...") print(f" Nano terms found: {', '.join(matching_nano_terms)}") print(f" URL: {link}") print() print(f"\n🎯 FILTERING RESULTS:") print(f"Total articles processed: {len(all_articles)}") print(f"Target articles identified: {len(target_articles)}") if len(target_articles) == 0: print("\n⚠️ No articles met all criteria. Let's analyze why...") # Diagnostic analysis has_2012 = sum(1 for a in all_articles if '2012' in f"{a.get('title', '').lower()} {a.get('snippet', '').lower()} {a.get('link', '').lower()}") has_sci_rep = sum(1 for a in all_articles if any(term in f"{a.get('title', '').lower()} {a.get('snippet', '').lower()} {a.get('link', '').lower()}" for term in ['scientific reports', 'sci rep', 'nature.com/srep'])) has_nano = sum(1 for a in all_articles if any(term in f"{a.get('title', '').lower()} {a.get('snippet', '').lower()} {a.get('link', '').lower()}" for term in nano_terms)) has_plasmons = sum(1 for a in all_articles if any(term in f"{a.get('title', '').lower()} {a.get('snippet', '').lower()} {a.get('link', '').lower()}" for term in plasmon_terms)) print(f"\n📊 DIAGNOSTIC BREAKDOWN:") print(f"Articles mentioning 2012: {has_2012}") print(f"Articles from Scientific Reports: {has_sci_rep}") print(f"Articles with nano-compounds: {has_nano}") print(f"Articles with plasmons (excluded): {has_plasmons}") # Show some sample articles for debugging print(f"\n🔍 SAMPLE ARTICLES FOR DEBUGGING:") for i, article in enumerate(all_articles[:3], 1): title = article.get('title', '') snippet = article.get('snippet', '') link = article.get('link', '') combined = f"{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()} {link.lower()}" print(f"\n Sample {i}:") print(f" Title: {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") print(f" Has 2012: {'2012' in combined}") print(f" Has Sci Rep: {any(term in combined for term in ['scientific reports', 'sci rep', 'nature.com/srep'])}") print(f" Has Nano: {any(term in combined for term in nano_terms)}") print(f" Has Plasmon: {any(term in combined for term in plasmon_terms)}") elif len(target_articles) < 23: print(f"\n⚠️ Found {len(target_articles)} articles, but PLAN mentions 23 target articles.") print(f"This might be due to strict filtering criteria or the search results may not contain all 23.") # Save the filtered results regardless of count timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S") target_file_output = f'workspace/scientific_reports_2012_filtered_articles_{timestamp}.json' output_data = { 'extraction_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'total_articles_processed': len(all_articles), 'target_articles_found': len(target_articles), 'filtering_criteria': { 'year': '2012', 'journal': 'Scientific Reports', 'content': 'nano-compounds', 'exclusion': 'no plasmon mentions' }, 'nano_terms_searched': nano_terms, 'plasmon_terms_excluded': plasmon_terms, 'target_articles': target_articles } with open(target_file_output, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(output_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"\n💾 Filtered results saved to: {target_file_output}") if target_articles: print(f"\n📋 TARGET ARTICLES SUMMARY:") print("-" * 80) for article in target_articles: print(f"{article['article_id']}. {article['title']}") print(f" Nano-compounds: {', '.join(article['matching_nano_terms'])}") print(f" URL: {article['link']}") print() print(f"\n🚀 NEXT STEP: Access full article content to identify specific nano-compounds studied") else: print(f"\n🔄 NEXT STEP: Review filtering criteria or search for additional article sources") else: print(f"❌ Error: File {target_file} not found") if os.path.exists('workspace'): print("Available files in workspace:") for file in os.listdir('workspace'): print(f" - {file}") else: print("Workspace directory not found")

Find which nano terms matched matching_nano_terms = [term for term in nano_terms if term in combined_text] target_articles.append({ 'article_id': len(target_articles) + 1, 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'source_query': article.get('source_query', ''), 'result_set': article.get('result_set', 0), 'matching_nano_terms': matching_nano_terms, 'criteria_met': { '2012': is_2012, 'scientific_reports': is_scientific_reports, 'nano_compound': has_nano_compound, 'no_plasmon': not has_plasmon } }) print(f"✅ Article {len(target_articles)}: {title[:60]}...") print(f" Nano terms found: {', '.join(matching_nano_terms)}") print(f" URL: {link}") print() print(f"\n🎯 FILTERING RESULTS:") print(f"Total articles processed: {len(all_articles)}") print(f"Target articles identified: {len(target_articles)}") if len(target_articles) == 0: print("\n⚠️ No articles met all criteria. Let's analyze why...") # Diagnostic analysis has_2012 = sum(1 for a in all_articles if '2012' in f"{a.get('title', '').lower()} {a.get('snippet', '').lower()} {a.get('link', '').lower()}") has_sci_rep = sum(1 for a in all_articles if any(term in f"{a.get('title', '').lower()} {a.get('snippet', '').lower()} {a.get('link', '').lower()}" for term in ['scientific reports', 'sci rep', 'nature.com/srep'])) has_nano = sum(1 for a in all_articles if any(term in f"{a.get('title', '').lower()} {a.get('snippet', '').lower()} {a.get('link', '').lower()}" for term in nano_terms)) has_plasmons = sum(1 for a in all_articles if any(term in f"{a.get('title', '').lower()} {a.get('snippet', '').lower()} {a.get('link', '').lower()}" for term in plasmon_terms)) print(f"\n📊 DIAGNOSTIC BREAKDOWN:") print(f"Articles mentioning 2012: {has_2012}") print(f"Articles from Scientific Reports: {has_sci_rep}") print(f"Articles with nano-compounds: {has_nano}") print(f"Articles with plasmons (excluded): {has_plasmons}") # Show some sample articles for debugging print(f"\n🔍 SAMPLE ARTICLES FOR DEBUGGING:") for i, article in enumerate(all_articles[:3], 1): title = article.get('title', '') snippet = article.get('snippet', '') link = article.get('link', '') combined = f"{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()} {link.lower()}" print(f"\n Sample {i}:") print(f" Title: {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") print(f" Has 2012: {'2012' in combined}") print(f" Has Sci Rep: {any(term in combined for term in ['scientific reports', 'sci rep', 'nature.com/srep'])}") print(f" Has Nano: {any(term in combined for term in nano_terms)}") print(f" Has Plasmon: {any(term in combined for term in plasmon_terms)}") elif len(target_articles) < 23: print(f"\n⚠️ Found {len(target_articles)} articles, but PLAN mentions 23 target articles.") print(f"This might be due to strict filtering criteria or the search results may not contain all 23.") # Save the filtered results regardless of count timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S") target_file_output = f'workspace/scientific_reports_2012_filtered_articles_{timestamp}.json' output_data = { 'extraction_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'total_articles_processed': len(all_articles), 'target_articles_found': len(target_articles), 'filtering_criteria': { 'year': '2012', 'journal': 'Scientific Reports', 'content': 'nano-compounds', 'exclusion': 'no plasmon mentions' }, 'nano_terms_searched': nano_terms, 'plasmon_terms_excluded': plasmon_terms, 'target_articles': target_articles } with open(target_file_output, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(output_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"\n💾 Filtered results saved to: {target_file_output}") if target_articles: print(f"\n📋 TARGET ARTICLES SUMMARY:") print("-" * 80) for article in target_articles: print(f"{article['article_id']}. {article['title']}") print(f" Nano-compounds: {', '.join(article['matching_nano_terms'])}") print(f" URL: {article['link']}") print() print(f"\n🚀 NEXT STEP: Access full article content to identify specific nano-compounds studied") else: print(f"\n🔄 NEXT STEP: Review filtering criteria or search for additional article sources") else: print(f"❌ Error: File {target_file} not found") if os.path.exists('workspace'): print("Available files in workspace:") for file in os.listdir('workspace'): print(f" - {file}") else: print("Workspace directory not found")

(total: {len(nano_terms)})") print(f"Plasmon terms (excluded): {plasmon_terms}") print(f"Scientific Reports indicators: {scientific_reports_terms[:3]}...") print("-" * 60) target_articles = [] for idx, article in enumerate(all_articles, 1): title = article.get('title', '') snippet = article.get('snippet', '') link = article.get('link', '') # Create combined text for analysis (proper variable scoping) title_lower = title.lower() snippet_lower = snippet.lower() link_lower = link.lower() combined_text = f"{title_lower} {snippet_lower} {link_lower}" # Save results timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S") output_file = f'workspace/scientific_reports_2012_target_articles_{timestamp}.json' output_data = { 'extraction_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'source_file': os.path.basename(target_file), 'total_articles_processed': len(all_articles), 'target_articles_found': len(target_articles), 'filtering_criteria': { 'year': '2012', 'journal': 'Scientific Reports', 'content_required': 'nano-compounds', 'content_excluded': 'plasmon mentions' }, 'search_terms': { 'nano_terms': nano_terms, 'plasmon_terms': plasmon_terms, 'journal_indicators': scientific_reports_terms }, 'target_articles': target_articles } with open(output_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(output_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"\n💾 Results saved to: {os.path.basename(output_file)}") if target_articles: print(f"\n📋 IDENTIFIED TARGET ARTICLES:") print("-" * 80) for article in target_articles: print(f"{article['article_id']}. {article['title']}") print(f" Nano-compounds: {', '.join(article['matching_nano_terms'])}") print(f" URL: {article['link']}") print() print(f"\n🚀 NEXT STEP: Access full article content to identify specific nano-compounds") else: print(f"\n🔄 RECOMMENDATION: Adjust filtering criteria or search additional sources") else: print(f"❌ Error: File {target_file} not found") if os.path.exists('workspace'): print("Available files in workspace:") for file in os.listdir('workspace'): print(f" - {file}") else: print("Workspace directory not found")

Save results timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S") output_file = f'workspace/scientific_reports_2012_target_articles_{timestamp}.json' output_data = { 'extraction_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'source_file': os.path.basename(target_file), 'total_articles_processed': len(all_articles), 'target_articles_found': len(target_articles), 'filtering_criteria': { 'year': '2012', 'journal': 'Scientific Reports', 'content_required': 'nano-compounds', 'content_excluded': 'plasmon mentions' }, 'search_terms': { 'nano_terms': nano_terms, 'plasmon_terms': plasmon_terms, 'journal_indicators': scientific_reports_terms }, 'target_articles': target_articles } with open(output_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(output_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"\n💾 Results saved to: {os.path.basename(output_file)}") if target_articles: print(f"\n📋 IDENTIFIED TARGET ARTICLES:") print("-" * 80) for article in target_articles: print(f"{article['article_id']}. {article['title']}") print(f" Nano-compounds: {', '.join(article['matching_nano_terms'])}") print(f" URL: {article['link']}") print() print(f"\n🚀 NEXT STEP: Access full article content to identify specific nano-compounds") else: print(f"\n🔄 RECOMMENDATION: Adjust filtering criteria or search additional sources") else: print(f"❌ Error: File {target_file} not found") if os.path.exists('workspace'): print("Available files in workspace:") for file in os.listdir('workspace'): print(f" - {file}") else: print("Workspace directory not found")

import os import json from datetime import datetime # Fix the variable scope issue by properly defining variables before using them in generator expressions print("Loading and filtering Scientific Reports 2012 articles...") print("=" * 80) target_file = 'workspace/nature_scientific_reports_2012_search_results_20250806_163939.json' if os.path.exists(target_file): with open(target_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: search_data = json.load(f) print(f"✅ Successfully loaded: {os.path.basename(target_file)}") print(f"Total queries executed: {search_data.get('total_queries', 'N/A')}") print(f"Total results found: {search_data.get('total_results', 'N/A')}") # Extract detailed results detailed_results = search_data.get('detailed_results', []) print(f"\n📊 Processing {len(detailed_results)} result sets...") # Collect all articles all_articles = [] for i, result_set in enumerate(detailed_results, 1): query = result_set.get('query', 'Unknown query') results = result_set.get('results', []) print(f" Result Set {i}: {len(results)} articles from query: {query[:50]}...") for article in results: article_with_context = article.copy() article_with_context['source_query'] = query article_with_context['result_set'] = i all_articles.append(article_with_context) print(f"\n📚 TOTAL ARTICLES COLLECTED: {len(all_articles)}") # Define search terms outside the loop to avoid scope issues nano_terms = [ 'nano', 'nanoparticle', 'nanoscale', 'nanotube', 'nanostructure', 'nanocomposite', 'nanomaterial', 'quantum dot', 'graphene', 'nanocrystal', 'nanowire', 'nanorod', 'nanosheet', 'fullerene' ] plasmon_terms = ['plasmon', 'plasmonic'] scientific_reports_terms = [ 'scientific reports', 'sci rep', 'nature.com/srep', 'nature.com/articles/srep', 'nature.com/subjects' ] print(f"\n🔍 FILTERING CRITERIA:") print(f"✅ Must contain: 2012 + Scientific Reports + nano-compounds") print(f"❌ Must NOT contain: plasmon/plasmonic terms") print("-" * 60) target_articles = [] # Process each article with proper variable scoping for idx, article in enumerate(all_articles, 1): title = article.get('title', '') snippet = article.get('snippet', '') link = article.get('link', '') # Create combined text BEFORE using it in any expressions title_text = title.lower() if title else '' snippet_text = snippet.lower() if snippet else '' link_text = link.lower() if link else '' combined_text = f"{title_text} {snippet_text} {link_text}" # Now apply filtering criteria with properly scoped variables is_2012 = '2012' in combined_text # Check for Scientific Reports indicators is_scientific_reports = False for term in scientific_reports_terms: if term in combined_text: is_scientific_reports = True break # Check for nano-compound terms has_nano_compound = False matching_nano_terms = [] for term in nano_terms: if term in combined_text: has_nano_compound = True matching_nano_terms.append(term) # Check for plasmon terms (we want articles WITHOUT these) has_plasmon = False for term in plasmon_terms: if term in combined_text: has_plasmon = True break # Article meets criteria if: 2012 + Scientific Reports + nano-compounds + NO plasmons meets_criteria = is_2012 and is_scientific_reports and has_nano_compound and not has_plasmon if meets_criteria: target_articles.append({ 'article_id': len(target_articles) + 1, 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'source_query': article.get('source_query', ''), 'result_set': article.get('result_set', 0), 'matching_nano_terms': matching_nano_terms, 'criteria_analysis': { '2012': is_2012, 'scientific_reports': is_scientific_reports, 'nano_compound': has_nano_compound, 'no_plasmon': not has_plasmon } }) print(f"✅ Target Article {len(target_articles)}:") print(f" Title: {title[:70]}...") print(f" Nano terms: {', '.join(matching_nano_terms)}") print(f" URL: {link}") print() print(f"\n" + "=" * 80) print(f"FILTERING RESULTS") print(f"=" * 80) print(f"Total articles processed: {len(all_articles)}") print(f"Target articles identified: {len(target_articles)}") # If no articles found, run diagnostic analysis if len(target_articles) == 0: print(f"\n⚠️ No articles met all criteria. Running diagnostic analysis...") # Count articles meeting individual criteria stats = { 'has_2012': 0, 'has_sci_rep': 0, 'has_nano': 0, 'has_plasmon': 0, 'meets_partial': 0 } for article in all_articles: title = article.get('title', '').lower() snippet = article.get('snippet', '').lower() link = article.get('link', '').lower() text = f"{title} {snippet} {link}" has_2012 = '2012' in text has_sci_rep = any(term in text for term in scientific_reports_terms) has_nano = any(term in text for term in nano_terms) has_plasmon = any(term in text for term in plasmon_terms) if has_2012: stats['has_2012'] += 1 if has_sci_rep: stats['has_sci_rep'] += 1 if has_nano: stats['has_nano'] += 1 if has_plasmon: stats['has_plasmon'] += 1 if has_2012 and has_sci_rep: stats['meets_partial'] += 1 print(f"\n📊 DIAGNOSTIC BREAKDOWN:") print(f"Articles mentioning 2012: {stats['has_2012']}/{len(all_articles)}") print(f"Articles from Scientific Reports: {stats['has_sci_rep']}/{len(all_articles)}") print(f"Articles with nano-compounds: {stats['has_nano']}/{len(all_articles)}") print(f"Articles with plasmons (excluded): {stats['has_plasmon']}/{len(all_articles)}") print(f"Articles meeting 2012 + Sci Rep: {stats['meets_partial']}/{len(all_articles)}") # Show sample articles for debugging print(f"\n🔍 SAMPLE ARTICLES FOR DEBUGGING:") for i in range(min(5, len(all_articles))): article = all_articles[i] title = article.get('title', '') link = article.get('link', '') text = f"{title.lower()} {article.get('snippet', '').lower()} {link.lower()}" print(f"\n Sample {i+1}:") print(f" Title: {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") print(f" ✓ 2012: {'2012' in text}") print(f" ✓ Sci Rep: {any(term in text for term in scientific_reports_terms)}") print(f" ✓ Nano: {any(term in text for term in nano_terms)}") print(f" ❌ Plasmon: {any(term in text for term in plasmon_terms)}") # Save results regardless of count timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S") output_file = f'workspace/scientific_reports_2012_filtered_articles_{timestamp}.json' output_data = { 'extraction_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'source_file': os.path.basename(target_file), 'total_articles_processed': len(all_articles), 'target_articles_found': len(target_articles), 'filtering_criteria': { 'year': '2012', 'journal': 'Scientific Reports', 'content_required': 'nano-compounds', 'content_excluded': 'plasmon mentions' }, 'search_terms_used': { 'nano_terms': nano_terms, 'plasmon_terms': plasmon_terms, 'journal_indicators': scientific_reports_terms }, 'target_articles': target_articles } with open(output_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(output_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"\n💾 Results saved to: {os.path.basename(output_file)}") if target_articles: print(f"\n📋 IDENTIFIED TARGET ARTICLES:") print("-" * 80) for article in target_articles: print(f"{article['article_id']}. {article['title']}") print(f" Nano-compounds: {', '.join(article['matching_nano_terms'])}") print(f" URL: {article['link']}") print() print(f"\n🚀 READY FOR NEXT STEP: Access full article content to identify specific nano-compounds") print(f"Note: Found {len(target_articles)} articles. PLAN mentions 23 target articles.") print(f"This discrepancy may be due to search limitations or strict filtering criteria.") else: print(f"\n🔄 RECOMMENDATION: The search results may not contain the specific 23 articles") print(f"mentioned in the PLAN. Consider adjusting search terms or accessing articles directly.") else: print(f"❌ Error: File {target_file} not found") if os.path.exists('workspace'): print("Available files in workspace:") for file in os.listdir('workspace'): print(f" - {file}") else: print("Workspace directory not found")

import os import json from datetime import datetime # Fix the variable scope issue by properly defining variables before using them in generator expressions print("Loading and filtering Scientific Reports 2012 articles...") print("=" * 80) target_file = 'workspace/nature_scientific_reports_2012_search_results_20250806_163939.json' if os.path.exists(target_file): with open(target_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: search_data = json.load(f) print(f"✅ Successfully loaded: {os.path.basename(target_file)}") print(f"Total queries executed: {search_data.get('total_queries', 'N/A')}") print(f"Total results found: {search_data.get('total_results', 'N/A')}") # Extract detailed results detailed_results = search_data.get('detailed_results', []) print(f"\n📊 Processing {len(detailed_results)} result sets...") # Collect all articles all_articles = [] for i, result_set in enumerate(detailed_results, 1): query = result_set.get('query', 'Unknown query') results = result_set.get('results', []) print(f" Result Set {i}: {len(results)} articles from query: {query[:50]}...") for article in results: article_with_context = article.copy() article_with_context['source_query'] = query article_with_context['result_set'] = i all_articles.append(article_with_context) print(f"\n📚 TOTAL ARTICLES COLLECTED: {len(all_articles)}") # Define search terms outside the loop to avoid scope issues nano_terms = [ 'nano', 'nanoparticle', 'nanoscale', 'nanotube', 'nanostructure', 'nanocomposite', 'nanomaterial', 'quantum dot', 'graphene', 'nanocrystal', 'nanowire', 'nanorod', 'nanosheet', 'fullerene' ] plasmon_terms = ['plasmon', 'plasmonic'] scientific_reports_terms = [ 'scientific reports', 'sci rep', 'nature.com/srep', 'nature.com/articles/srep', 'nature.com/subjects' ] print(f"\n🔍 FILTERING CRITERIA:") print(f"✅ Must contain: 2012 + Scientific Reports + nano-compounds") print(f"❌ Must NOT contain: plasmon/plasmonic terms") print("-" * 60) target_articles = [] # Process each article with proper variable scoping for idx, article in enumerate(all_articles, 1): title = article.get('title', '') snippet = article.get('snippet', '') link = article.get('link', '') # Create combined text BEFORE using it in any expressions title_text = title.lower() if title else '' snippet_text = snippet.lower() if snippet else '' link_text = link.lower() if link else '' combined_text = f"{title_text} {snippet_text} {link_text}" # Now apply filtering criteria with properly scoped variables is_2012 = '2012' in combined_text # Check for Scientific Reports indicators is_scientific_reports = False for term in scientific_reports_terms: if term in combined_text: is_scientific_reports = True break # Check for nano-compound terms has_nano_compound = False matching_nano_terms = [] for term in nano_terms: if term in combined_text: has_nano_compound = True matching_nano_terms.append(term) # Check for plasmon terms (we want articles WITHOUT these) has_plasmon = False for term in plasmon_terms: if term in combined_text: has_plasmon = True break # Article meets criteria if: 2012 + Scientific Reports + nano-compounds + NO plasmons meets_criteria = is_2012 and is_scientific_reports and has_nano_compound and not has_plasmon if meets_criteria: target_articles.append({ 'article_id': len(target_articles) + 1, 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'source_query': article.get('source_query', ''), 'result_set': article.get('result_set', 0), 'matching_nano_terms': matching_nano_terms, 'criteria_analysis': { '2012': is_2012, 'scientific_reports': is_scientific_reports, 'nano_compound': has_nano_compound, 'no_plasmon': not has_plasmon } }) print(f"✅ Target Article {len(target_articles)}:") print(f" Title: {title[:70]}...") print(f" Nano terms: {', '.join(matching_nano_terms)}") print(f" URL: {link}") print() print(f"\n" + "=" * 80) print(f"FILTERING RESULTS") print(f"=" * 80) print(f"Total articles processed: {len(all_articles)}") print(f"Target articles identified: {len(target_articles)}") # If no articles found, run diagnostic analysis if len(target_articles) == 0: print(f"\n⚠️ No articles met all criteria. Running diagnostic analysis...") # Count articles meeting individual criteria stats = { 'has_2012': 0, 'has_sci_rep': 0, 'has_nano': 0, 'has_plasmon': 0, 'meets_partial': 0 } for article in all_articles: title = article.get('title', '').lower() snippet = article.get('snippet', '').lower() link = article.get('link', '').lower() text = f"{title} {snippet} {link}" has_2012 = '2012' in text has_sci_rep = any(term in text for term in scientific_reports_terms) has_nano = any(term in text for term in nano_terms) has_plasmon = any(term in text for term in plasmon_terms) if has_2012: stats['has_2012'] += 1 if has_sci_rep: stats['has_sci_rep'] += 1 if has_nano: stats['has_nano'] += 1 if has_plasmon: stats['has_plasmon'] += 1 if has_2012 and has_sci_rep: stats['meets_partial'] += 1 print(f"\n📊 DIAGNOSTIC BREAKDOWN:") print(f"Articles mentioning 2012: {stats['has_2012']}/{len(all_articles)}") print(f"Articles from Scientific Reports: {stats['has_sci_rep']}/{len(all_articles)}") print(f"Articles with nano-compounds: {stats['has_nano']}/{len(all_articles)}") print(f"Articles with plasmons (excluded): {stats['has_plasmon']}/{len(all_articles)}") print(f"Articles meeting 2012 + Sci Rep: {stats['meets_partial']}/{len(all_articles)}") # Show sample articles for debugging print(f"\n🔍 SAMPLE ARTICLES FOR DEBUGGING:") for i in range(min(5, len(all_articles))): article = all_articles[i] title = article.get('title', '') link = article.get('link', '') text = f"{title.lower()} {article.get('snippet', '').lower()} {link.lower()}" print(f"\n Sample {i+1}:") print(f" Title: {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") print(f" ✓ 2012: {'2012' in text}") print(f" ✓ Sci Rep: {any(term in text for term in scientific_reports_terms)}") print(f" ✓ Nano: {any(term in text for term in nano_terms)}") print(f" ❌ Plasmon: {any(term in text for term in plasmon_terms)}") # Save results regardless of count timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S") output_file = f'workspace/scientific_reports_2012_filtered_articles_{timestamp}.json' output_data = { 'extraction_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'source_file': os.path.basename(target_file), 'total_articles_processed': len(all_articles), 'target_articles_found': len(target_articles), 'filtering_criteria': { 'year': '2012', 'journal': 'Scientific Reports', 'content_required': 'nano-compounds', 'content_excluded': 'plasmon mentions' }, 'search_terms_used': { 'nano_terms': nano_terms, 'plasmon_terms': plasmon_terms, 'journal_indicators': scientific_reports_terms }, 'target_articles': target_articles } with open(output_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(output_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f"\n💾 Results saved to: {os.path.basename(output_file)}") if target_articles: print(f"\n📋 IDENTIFIED TARGET ARTICLES:") print("-" * 80) for article in target_articles: print(f"{article['article_id']}. {article['title']}") print(f" Nano-compounds: {', '.join(article['matching_nano_terms'])}") print(f" URL: {article['link']}") print() print(f"\n🚀 READY FOR NEXT STEP: Access full article content to identify specific nano-compounds") print(f"Note: Found {len(target_articles)} articles. PLAN mentions 23 target articles.") print(f"This discrepancy may be due to search limitations or strict filtering criteria.") else: print(f"\n🔄 RECOMMENDATION: The search results may not contain the specific 23 articles") print(f"mentioned in the PLAN. Consider adjusting search terms or accessing articles directly.") else: print(f"❌ Error: File {target_file} not found") if os.path.exists('workspace'): print("Available files in workspace:") for file in os.listdir('workspace'): print(f" - {file}") else: print("Workspace directory not found")
